    2783             : #define YYABORT         goto yyabortlab
    2784             : #define YYERROR         goto yyerrorlab

    2787             : /* Like YYERROR except do call yyerror.  This remains here temporarily
    2788             :    to ease the transition to the new meaning of YYERROR, for GCC.
    2789             :    Once GCC version 2 has supplanted version 1, this can go.  */

    2792             : 
    2793             : #define YYRECOVERING()  (!!yyerrstatus)
    2794             : 
    2795             : #define YYBACKUP(Token, Value)                                  \
    2796             : do                                                              \
    2797             :   if (yychar == YYEMPTY && yylen == 1)                          \
    2798             :     {                                                           \
    2799             :       yychar = (Token);                                         \
    2800             :       yylval = (Value);                                         \
    2801             :       yytoken = YYTRANSLATE (yychar);                           \
    2802             :       YYPOPSTACK (1);                                           \
    2803             :       goto yybackup;                                            \
    2804             :     }                                                           \
    2805             :   else                                                          \
    2806             :     {                                                           \
    2807             :       yyerror (parser, scanner, YY_("syntax error: cannot back up")); \
    2808             :       YYERROR;                                                  \
    2809             :     }                                                           \
    2810             : while (YYID (0))

    2813             : #define YYTERROR        1
    2814             : #define YYERRCODE       256
    2815             : 
    2816             : 
    2817             : /* YYLLOC_DEFAULT -- Set CURRENT to span from RHS[1] to RHS[N].
    2818             :    If N is 0, then set CURRENT to the empty location which ends
    2819             :    the previous symbol: RHS[0] (always defined).  */
    2820             : 
    2821             : #define YYRHSLOC(Rhs, K) ((Rhs)[K])
    2822             : #ifndef YYLLOC_DEFAULT
    2823             : # define YYLLOC_DEFAULT(Current, Rhs, N)                                \
    2824             :     do                                                                  \
    2825             :       if (YYID (N))                                                    \
    2826             :         {                                                               \
    2827             :           (Current).first_line   = YYRHSLOC (Rhs, 1).first_line;        \
    2828             :           (Current).first_column = YYRHSLOC (Rhs, 1).first_column;      \
    2829             :           (Current).last_line    = YYRHSLOC (Rhs, N).last_line;         \
    2830             :           (Current).last_column  = YYRHSLOC (Rhs, N).last_column;       \
    2831             :         }                                                               \
    2832             :       else                                                              \
    2833             :         {                                                               \
    2834             :           (Current).first_line   = (Current).last_line   =              \
